focus_tree = {
	id = BEL_focus_tree
	
	country = {
		factor = 0
		
		modifier = {
			add = 10
			tag = BEL 
		}

		modifier = {
			add = 10
			original_tag = BEL
		}
	}	

	default = no

	continuous_focus_position = { x = 20000 y = 20000 }

	#########################
	### TOMBOY ACCEPTANCE ###
	#########################

	# Popularize Tomboyism
	focus = {
		id = BEL_acceptance_popularize
		icon = GFX_goal_generic_improve_relations

		cost = 2

		search_filters = { category_tomboy_acceptance }

		x = 2
		y = 0

		completion_reward = {
			add_to_variable = {
				var = tomboy_acceptance_lvl
				value = 1
				tooltip = tomboy_acceptance_lvl_tt
			}
			add_political_power = 50
		}
	}

	# Pass pro-Tomboy Legislation
	focus = {
		id = BEL_acceptance_legislation
		icon = GFX_goal_bel_tomboy_acceptance_1

		cost = 2

		search_filters = { category_tomboy_acceptance }

		x = 1
		y = 1

		prerequisite = {
			focus = BEL_acceptance_popularize
		}

		completion_reward = {
			add_to_variable = {
				var = tomboy_acceptance_lvl
				value = 1
				tooltip = tomboy_acceptance_lvl_tt
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = BEL_idea_acceptance_none
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = BEL_idea_acceptance_none
					add_idea = BEL_idea_acceptance_low
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = BEL_idea_acceptance_low
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = BEL_idea_acceptance_low
					add_idea = BEL_idea_acceptance_low_med
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = BEL_idea_acceptance_low_med
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = BEL_idea_acceptance_low_med
					add_idea = BEL_idea_acceptance_medium
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = BEL_idea_acceptance_medium
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = BEL_idea_acceptance_medium
					add_idea = BEL_idea_acceptance_medium_high
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = BEL_idea_acceptance_medium_high
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = BEL_idea_acceptance_medium_high
					add_idea = BEL_idea_acceptance_high
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = BEL_idea_acceptance_high
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = BEL_idea_acceptance_high
					add_idea = BEL_idea_acceptance_high_high
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = BEL_idea_acceptance_high_high
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = BEL_idea_acceptance_high_high
					add_idea = BEL_idea_acceptance_absolute
				}
			}
		}
	}

	# Integrate Tomboys into Workplaces
	focus = {
		id = BEL_acceptance_work
		icon = GFX_goal_bel_tomboy_acceptance_2

		cost = 2

		search_filters = { category_tomboy_acceptance }

		x = 3
		y = 1

		prerequisite = {
			focus = BEL_acceptance_popularize
		}

		completion_reward = {
			random_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_by = BEL
					is_controlled_by = BEL
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				var = tomboy_acceptance_lvl
				value = 1
				tooltip = tomboy_acceptance_lvl_tt
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = BEL_idea_acceptance_none
				}

				}
			}

				}

				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = BEL_idea_acceptance_high

				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {

				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = BEL_idea_acceptance_high_high
					add_idea = BEL_idea_acceptance_absolute
				}
			}
		}

	# Open Political Sphere
	focus = {
		id = BEL_open_political_sphere
		icon = GFX_goal_generic_improve_relations

		cost = 1

		x = 12
		y = 0

		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL Monarchist Fascist Monafash Communist Democracy}

		allow_branch = {
			OR = {
				has_completed_focus = BEL_acceptance_supremacy
				is_debug = yes
			}
		}

		completion_reward = {
			add_political_power = 150
			remove_ideas = BEL_disorganised_nation
		}
	}

	# Crack down on Democracy
	focus = {
		id = BEL_political_crack_down
		icon = GFX_goal_bel_big_royal

		cost = 4

		x = 10
		y = 1

		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL Monarchist Fascist Monafash }

		prerequisite = {
			focus = BEL_open_political_sphere
		}

		mutually_exclusive = {
			focus = BEL_political_promote
		}

		completion_reward = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_government = fascism
						has_government = communism
						has_government = neutrality
						tag = BEL
					}
				}
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = BEL
					modifier = small_decrease
				}
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = democratic
				popularity = -0.1
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communism
				popularity = -0.1
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = fascism
				popularity = 0.1
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = neutrality
				popularity = 0.1
			}
			add_stability = -0.25
			mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
			custom_effect_tooltip = BEL_political_antidem_tt
		}
	}

	# The Monarch alone
	focus = {
		id = BEL_monarchism_the_monarch_alone
		icon = GFX_goal_bel_monarchism_lalatina

		cost = 4

		x = 8
		y = 2

		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL Monarchist }
		
		allow_branch = {
			AND = {
				NOT = {
					has_completed_focus = BEL_monafash_monarchist_fascist_alliance
				}
				has_completed_focus = BEL_acceptance_supremacy
				has_completed_focus = BEL_political_crack_down
			}
		}

		prerequisite = {
			focus = BEL_political_crack_down
		}

		available = {
			OR = {
				has_government = fascism
				has_government = neutrality
			}
		}

		mutually_exclusive = {
			focus = BEL_monafash_monarchist_fascist_alliance
			focus = BEL_fascism_fascist_ascendance
		}

		completion_reward = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = neutrality
				popularity = 0.1
			}
			add_stability = -0.1

			focus = BEL_monarchism_the_monarch_alone
		}

			OR = {
				has_completed_focus = BEL_monarchism_the_monarch_alone
				#is_debug = yes
			}
		}

			add_popularity = {
				ideology = democratic
				popularity = -0.05
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communism
				popularity = -0.05
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = fascism
				popularity = -0.05
			}
			add_stability = -0.1
		}
	}

	# Prepare an Army

	# Demand Tomboy-Managed referendums in Netherlands and Luxembourg
	focus = {
		id = BEL_monarchism_demand_referendums
		icon = tbd

		cost = 5
		
		x = 8
		y = 9

		prerequisite = {
			focus = BEL_monarchism_prepare_army
		}

		available = {
			is_subject = no
			has_army_manpower = { size > 149999 } # 150k
		}

		mutually_exclusive = {
			focus = BEL_monarchism_subjugate_for_safety
			focus = BEL_monarchism_propose_protective_alliance
		}

		bypass = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					HOL = {
						OR = {
							exists = no
							is_puppet_of = BEL
						}
					}
					LUX = {
						OR = {
							exists = no
							is_puppet_of = BEL
						}
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_war_with = HOL
					has_war_with = LUX
				}
			}
		}
		
		completion_reward = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					HOL = {
						exists = yes
						NOT = {
							is_puppet_of = BEL # If not at war, and not a puppet, and exists, send event
						}
						has_war = no
					}
				}
				HOL = {
					country_event = tomboy.1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					LUX = {
						exists = yes
						NOT = {
							is_puppet_of = BEL # If not at war, and not a puppet, and exists, send event
						}
						has_war = no
					}
				}
				LUX = {
					country_event = tomboy.1
				}
			}

			# If at war:
			if = {
				limit = {
					HOL = {
						exists = yes
						NOT = {
							is_puppet_of = BEL # If at war, not a puppet, and exists, just create wargoal
						}
						has_war = yes
					}
				}
				BEL = {
					create_wargoal = {
						target = HOL
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					LUX = {
						exists = yes
						NOT = {
							is_puppet_of = BEL # If at war, not a puppet, and exists, just create wargoal
						}
						has_war = yes
					}
				}
				BEL = {
					create_wargoal = {
						target = LUX
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
			}

			custom_effect_tooltip = BEL_warring_wont_be_asked_tt
		}
	}

	# Propose protective alliance (Monarchist countries only!)
	focus = {
		id = BEL_monarchism_propose_protective_alliance
		icon = tbd

		cost = 5
		
		x = 10
		y = 9

		prerequisite = {
			focus = BEL_monarchism_prepare_army
		}

		mutually_exclusive = {
			focus = BEL_monarchism_demand_referendums
			focus = BEL_monarchism_subjugate_for_safety
		}

		available = {
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = HOL
				has_war_with = LUX
			}
			HOL = {
				has_war = no
			}
			LUX = {
				has_war = no
			}
			OR = {
				HOL = {
					AND = {
						has_government = neutrality
						is_in_faction = no # Would be weird to allow this to run if both are in factions already.
					}
				}
				LUX = {
					AND = {
						has_government = neutrality
						is_in_faction = no
					}
				}
			}
			OR = {
				is_in_faction = no
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
		}

		bypass = {
			HOL = {
				OR = {
					exists = no
					is_puppet_of = BEL
					is_in_faction_with = BEL
				}
			}
			LUX = {
				OR = {
					exists = no
					is_puppet_of = BEL
					is_in_faction_with = BEL
				}
			}
		}
		
		completion_reward = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction = no
				}
				create_faction = BEL_monarchism_monarchist_protection_faction
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						HOL = {
							has_government = neutrality
							is_in_faction = no
						}
					}
					HOL = {
						country_event = tomboy.5
					}
				}
				else = { # I didn't expect PDX to know what if-else is
					create_wargoal = {
						target = HOL
						type = puppet_wargoal_focus
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						LUX = {
							has_government = neutrality
							is_in_faction = no
						}
					}
					LUX = {
						country_event = tomboy.5
					}
				}
				else = {
					create_wargoal = {
						target = HOL
						type = puppet_wargoal_focus
					}
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = invite_monarchist_nations_tt
		}
	}

	# Prepare Maginot sabotage

		id = BEL_monarchism_france_offense_sabotage_maginot
		icon = tbd

		cost = 5
		
		x = 12
		y = 13

		prerequisite = {
			focus = BEL_monarchism_france_offense_focus_on_offense
		}

		available = {
			OR = {
				intel_level_over = {
					target = FRA
					civilian_intel > 0.2 
				}
				intel_level_over = {
					target = FRA
					army_intel > 0.15
				}
				FRA = {
					OR = {
						exists = no
						is_puppet_of = BEL
						is_in_faction_with = BEL
					}
				}
			}
		}

		bypass = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					28 = { # Alsace-Lorraine
						bunker < 15
					}
					18 = { # Champagne
						bunker < 7
					}
					785 = { # Picardy
						bunker < 3
					}
					29 = { # Nord-Pas-De-Calais
						bunker < 7
					}
				}
				FRA = {
					OR = {
						exists = no
						is_puppet_of = BEL
						is_in_faction_with = BEL
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		completion_reward = {
			hidden_effect = {
				set_country_flag = BEL_sabotaged_maginot
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = BEL_monarchism_france_offense_sabotage_maginot_reward_tt

	focus = {
		id = BEL_monarchism_germany_justice_anti-tank
		icon = tbd

		cost = 5
		
		x = 19
		y = 15

		prerequisite = {
			focus = BEL_monarchism_germany_justice_assert_eastern_claims
			focus = BEL_monarchism_germany_justice_rekindle_monarchism
		}

		bypass = {

			OR = {
				has_tech = advanced_light_tank_chassis

				has_tech = advanced_light_tank
				has_tech = main_battle_tank
			}
		}
		
		completion_reward = {
			add_tech_bonus = {
				category = cat_anti_tank
				bonus = 2
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dlc = "No Step Back"
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_tech = advanced_medium_tank_chassis
							has_tech = advanced_heavy_tank_chassis
						}
						NOT = {
							has_tech = main_battle_tank_chassis
						}
					}
					add_tech_bonus = {
						technology = main_battle_tank_chassis
						bonus = 1
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_tech = improved_light_tank_chassis
						NOT = {
							has_tech = advanced_light_tank_chassis
						}
					}
					add_tech_bonus = {
						technology = advanced_light_tank_chassis
						bonus = 1
					}
				}
				else = {
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = modern_tank_chassis_1
						amount = 150
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = light_tank_chassis_3
						amount = 150
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_tech = advanced_medium_tank
							has_tech = advanced_heavy_tank
						}
						NOT = {
							has_tech = main_battle_tank
						}
					}
					add_tech_bonus = {
						technology = main_battle_tank
						bonus = 1
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_tech = improved_light_tank
						NOT = {
							has_tech = advanced_light_tank
						}
					}
					add_tech_bonus = {
						technology = advanced_light_tank
						bonus = 1
					}
				}
				else = {
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = modern_tank_destroyer_equipment_1
						amount = 150
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = light_tank_destroyer_equipment_3
						amount = 150
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	# Attempt a peaceful resolution
	focus = {
		id = BEL_monafash_imperialism_benelux_attempt_peace
		icon = tbd

		cost = 5
		
		x = 15
		y = 12

		prerequisite = {
			focus = BEL_monafash_imperialism_homefront_declare_our_plans
		}

		mutually_exclusive = {
			focus = BEL_monafash_imperialism_benelux_demand_hol_lux
		}

		bypass = {
			owns_state = 35
			owns_state = 7
			owns_state = 36
			owns_state = 8
		}

		available = {
			OR = {
				HOL = {
					exists = yes
				}
				LUX = {
					exists = yes
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = HOL
				has_war_with = LUX
			}
		}
		
		completion_reward = {
			add_power_balance_value = {
				id = BEL_bop_monafash
				value = 0.1
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					HOL = {
						has_government = LUX
					}
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = HOL
					popularity = 0.05
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = HOL
					popularity = 0.025
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = LUX
					popularity = 0.025
				}
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = HOL
				modifier = BEL_friendly_interaction
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = LUX
				modifier = BEL_friendly_interaction
			}
			HOL = {
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = BEL
					modifier = BEL_friendly_interaction
				}
			}
			LUX = {
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = BEL

				}

	# Poke the Hornets Nest
	focus = {
		id = BEL_monafash_imperialism_benelux_hol_poke_hornets_nest
		icon = tbd

		cost = 5
		
		x = 16
		y = 14

		prerequisite = {
			focus = BEL_monafash_imperialism_benelux_hol_aid_tomboys
		}

		bypass = {
			HOL = {
				exists = no
				NOT = {
					is_puppet_of = BEL
				}
			}
			has_war_with = HOL
		}
		
		completion_reward = {
			HOL = {
				add_stability = -0.25
				every_core_state = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							arms_factory > 1
						}
						damage_building = {
							type = arms_factory
							damage = 7 # Maximum is 8
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							industrial_complex > 1
						}
						damage_building = {
							type = industrial_complex
							damage = 4 # Maximum is 5
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							air_base > 1
						}
						damage_building = {
							type = air_base
							damage = 0.95 # Maximum is 1
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							dockyard > 1
						}
						damage_building = {
							type = dockyard
							damage = 4 # Maximum is 5
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							naval_base > 1
						}
						damage_building = {
							type = naval_base
							damage = 0.75 # Maximum is 1
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	# Launch a surprise attack!
	focus = {
		id = BEL_monafash_imperialism_benelux_surprise_attack
		icon = tbd

		cost = 5
		
		x = 13
		y = 16

		prerequisite = {
			focus = BEL_monafash_imperialism_benelux_demand_hol_lux
			focus = BEL_monafash_imperialism_benelux_lux_propose_union
			focus = BEL_monafash_imperialism_benelux_hol_offer_way_out
		}

		mutually_exclusive = {
			focus = BEL_monafash_imperialism_benelux_unify
		}

		bypass = {
			OR = {
				has_war_with = HOL
				HOL = {
					exists = no
					is_puppet_of = BEL
				}
			}
			OR = {
				has_war_with = LUX
				LUX = {
					exists = no
					is_puppet_of = BEL
				}
			}
		}

		will_lead_to_war_with = HOL
		will_lead_to_war_with = LUX
		
		completion_reward = {
			add_power_balance_value = {
				id = BEL_bop_monafash
				value = -0.05
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					HOL = {
						exists = yes
						NOT = {
							has_war_with = BEL
							is_puppet_of = BEL
							is_ally_with = BEL
						}
					}
				}
				create_wargoal = {
					target = HOL
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					LUX = {
						exists = yes
						NOT = {
							has_war_with = BEL
							is_puppet_of = BEL
							is_ally_with = BEL
						}
					}
				}
				create_wargoal = {
					target = LUX
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = BEL_idea_benelux_surprise_attack
				months = 2
			}
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = conquer
				id = HOL
				value = 50
			}
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = conquer
				id = LUX
				value = 50
			}
		}
	}

	# Unify the Benelux
	focus = {
		id = BEL_monafash_imperialism_benelux_unify
		icon = tbd

		cost = 5
		
		x = 15
		y = 16

		prerequisite = {
			focus = BEL_monafash_imperialism_benelux_lux_propose_union
			focus = BEL_monafash_imperialism_benelux_hol_offer_way_out
		}

		mutually_exclusive = {
			focus = BEL_monafash_imperialism_benelux_surprise_attack
		}

		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				AND = {
					BEL = {
						AND = {
							owns_state = 35
							owns_state = 7
							owns_state = 36
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							HOL = {
								is_puppet_of = BEL
							}
						}
						HOL = {
							OR = {
								has_autonomy_state = autonomy_selfgoverning_territory
								has_autonomy_state = autonomy_freestate
							}
						}
					}
				}
				tooltip = BEL_monafash_imperialism_benelux_unify_HOL_trigger_tt
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				AND = {
					BEL = {
						owns_state = 8
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							LUX = {
								is_puppet_of = BEL
							}
						}
						LUX = {
							OR = {
								has_autonomy_state = autonomy_selfgoverning_territory
								has_autonomy_state = autonomy_freestate
							}
						}
					}
				}
				tooltip = BEL_monafash_imperialism_benelux_unify_LUX_trigger_tt
			}
		}
		
		completion_reward = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = fascism
				}
				add_power_balance_value = {
					id = BEL_bop_monafash
					value = 0.05
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_power_balance_value = {
					id = BEL_bop_monafash
					value = -0.05
				}
			}
			add_stability = 0.1
			add_war_support = 0.2
			if = {
				limit = {
					BEL = {
						owns_state = 35
					}
				}
				add_state_core = 35
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					BEL = {
						owns_state = 7
					}
				}
				add_state_core = 7
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					BEL = {
						owns_state = 36
					}
				}
				add_state_core = 36
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					BEL = {
						owns_state = 8
					}
				}
				add_state_core = 8
			}
		}
	}

	# Euronia
	focus = {
		id = BEL_monafash_imperialism_euronia
		icon = tbd

		cost = 5
		
		x = 13
		y = 19

		prerequisite = {
			focus = BEL_monafash_imperialism_germany_germania
		}
		prerequisite = {
			focus = BEL_monafash_imperialism_france_claim_marianne
		}
		prerequisite = {
			focus = BEL_monafash_imperialism_britain_britannia
		}
		prerequisite = {
			focus = BEL_monafash_imperialism_benelux_integrate_our_investments
		}
		prerequisite = {
			focus = BEL_monafash_imperialism_east_bulwark
		}
		
		completion_reward = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = fascism
				}
				add_power_balance_value = {
					id = BEL_bop_monafash
					value = 0.25
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_power_balance_value = {
					id = BEL_bop_monafash
					value = -0.25
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = BEL_idea_celebrating_marianne
				}
				remove_ideas = BEL_idea_celebrating_marianne
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = BEL_idea_celebrating_britannia
				}
				remove_ideas = BEL_idea_celebrating_britannia
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = BEL_idea_celebrating_germania
				}
				remove_ideas = BEL_idea_celebrating_germania
			}

			add_ideas = BEL_idea_euronia
		}
	}

		y = 14

			focus = BEL_monafash_imperialism_east_poland_instigate_an_attack

			focus = BEL_monafash_imperialism_east_poland_unite
		}

		available = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_completed_focus = BEL_monafash_imperialism_east_poland_instigate_an_attack
					has_completed_focus = BEL_monafash_imperialism_east_poland_war_with_poland
				}
				has_completed_focus = BEL_monafash_imperialism_east_poland_unite
			}
		}
		
		completion_reward = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = fascism
				}
				add_power_balance_value = {
					id = BEL_bop_monafash
					value = 0.15
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_power_balance_value = {
					id = BEL_bop_monafash
					value = -0.05
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = POL
					owner = {
						OR = {
							original_tag = BEL
							is_puppet_of = BEL
						}
					}
				}
				owner = {
					add_state_core = PREV # Puppets also get it cored
				}
				remove_core_of = POL # Bye-bye Poland!
			}
		}
	}

	# The Bulwark against the East
	focus = {
		id = BEL_monafash_imperialism_east_bulwark
		icon = tbd

		x = 24
		y = 17

		}

		available = {
			OR = {
				is_neighbor_of = SOV
				is_neighbor_of = UKR
				is_neighbor_of = BLR
				AND = {
					is_neighbor_of = LIT
					LIT = {
						has_government = communism
					}
				}
				AND = {
					is_neighbor_of = LAT
					LAT = {
						has_government = communism
					}
				}
				AND = {
					is_neighbor_of = EST
					EST = {
						has_government = communism
					}
				}
				AND = {
					is_neighbor_of = ROM
					ROM = {
						has_government = communism
					}
				}
				AND = {
					is_neighbor_of = HUN
					HUN = {
						has_government = communism
					}
				}
				AND = {
					is_neighbor_of = YUG
					YUG = {
						has_government = communism
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		completion_reward = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = fascism
				}
				add_power_balance_value = {
					id = BEL_bop_monafash
					value = 0.05
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_power_balance_value = {
					id = BEL_bop_monafash
					value = -0.05
				}
			}
			add_ideas = BEL_idea_iron_curtain
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						owner = {
							OR = {
								original_tag = BEL
								is_puppet_of = BEL
								is_ally_with = BEL
							}
						}
						any_neighbor_state = {
							owner = {
								OR = {
									original_tag = SOV
									original_tag = UKR
									original_tag = BLR
									AND = {
										original_tag = LIT
										has_government = communism
									}
									AND = {
										original_tag = LIT
										has_government = communism
									}
									AND = {
										original_tag = LAT
										has_government = communism
									}
									AND = {
										original_tag = EST
										has_government = communism
									}
									AND = {
										original_tag = ROM
										has_government = communism
									}
									AND = {
										original_tag = HUN
										has_government = communism
									}
									AND = {
										original_tag = YUG
										has_government = communism
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = bunker
					level = 4
					instant_build = yes
					province = {
						all_provinces = yes
						limit_to_border_country = SOV
					}
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = bunker
					level = 4
					instant_build = yes
					province = {
						all_provinces = yes
						limit_to_border_country = UKR
					}
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = bunker
					level = 4
					instant_build = yes
					province = {
						all_provinces = yes
						limit_to_border_country = BLR
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						LIT = {
							exists = yes
							has_government = communism
						}
					}
					add_building_construction = {
						type = bunker
						level = 4
						instant_build = yes
						province = {
							all_provinces = yes
							limit_to_border_country = LIT
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						LAT = {
							exists = yes
							has_government = communism
						}
					}
					add_building_construction = {
						type = bunker
						level = 4
						instant_build = yes
						province = {
							all_provinces = yes
							limit_to_border_country = LAT
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						EST = {

					add_building_construction = {

				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_tech = improved_light_tank
						NOT = {
							has_tech = advanced_light_tank
						}
					}
					add_tech_bonus = {
						technology = advanced_light_tank
						bonus = 1.75
						uses = 1
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_tech = basic_light_tank
						NOT = {
							has_tech = improved_light_tank
						}
					}
					add_tech_bonus = {
						technology = improved_light_tank
						bonus = 1.75
						uses = 1
					}
				}
				else = {
					add_tech_bonus = {
						technology = basic_light_tank
						bonus = 1.75
						uses = 1
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				random_list = {
					33 = {
						add_tech_bonus = {
							category = cat_light_armor
							bonus = 1.75
							uses = 1
						}
					}
					33 = {
						add_tech_bonus = {
							category = armor
							bonus = 1.75
							uses = 1
						}
					}
					33 = {
						if = {
							limit = {
								has_tech = armor_tech_4
							}
							army_experience = 150
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								has_tech = armor_tech_3
								NOT = {
									has_tech = armor_tech_4
								}
							}
							add_tech_bonus = {
								technology = armor_tech_4
								bonus = 1.75
								uses = 1
							}
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								has_tech = armor_tech_2
								NOT = {
									has_tech = armor_tech_3
								}
							}
							add_tech_bonus = {
								technology = armor_tech_3
								bonus = 1.75
								uses = 1
							}
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								has_tech = armor_tech_1
								NOT = {
									has_tech = armor_tech_2
								}
							}
							add_tech_bonus = {
								technology = armor_tech_2
								bonus = 1.75
								uses = 1
							}
						}
						else = {
							add_tech_bonus = {
								technology = armor_tech_1
								bonus = 1.75
								uses = 1
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
